SELECT c.customerid, c.firstname, c.lastname, CASE
    WHEN c.companyname = '' THEN (COALESCE(c.firstname, '') || ' ') || COALESCE(c.lastname, '')
    ELSE c.companyname
END, (c.companylogourl IS NULL) OR c.companylogourl = '', c.companylogourl, c.pannumber, c.gstnumber, c.companyemail, COALESCE(c.phone1, ''), COALESCE(c.address1, ''), COALESCE(c.zipcode, ''), p.paymenttermid IS NULL, p.paymenttermid, p.paymenttermname, c0.currencyid IS NULL, c0.currencyid, c0.currencyname, c1.cityid IS NULL, c1.cityid, c1.cityname, (
    SELECT count(*)::int
    FROM project AS p0
    WHERE c.customerid = p0.customerid), t."ProjectId", t."ProjectName", t."TotalEmployees", t."TotalAmount", t."ProjectStatus", t.statusid
FROM customer AS c
LEFT JOIN paymentterm AS p ON c.paymenttermid = p.paymenttermid
LEFT JOIN currency AS c0 ON c.currencyid = c0.currencyid
LEFT JOIN city AS c1 ON c.cityid = c1.cityid
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT p1.projectid AS "ProjectId", COALESCE(p1.projectname, '') AS "ProjectName", (
        SELECT count(*)::int
        FROM projectcontract AS p2
        INNER JOIN contractemployee AS c2 ON p2.contractid = c2.contractid
        WHERE p1.projectid = p2.projectid AND c2.categorysubstatusid IN (5, 6, 4, 3, 2) AND c2.contractid = COALESCE((
            SELECT p3.contractid
            FROM projectcontract AS p3
            WHERE p1.projectid = p3.projectid
            LIMIT 1), 0)) AS "TotalEmployees", (
        SELECT COALESCE(sum(p4.amount), 0.0)
        FROM projectcontract AS p4
        WHERE p1.projectid = p4.projectid) AS "TotalAmount", s.statusname AS "ProjectStatus", s.statusid, p1.customerid
    FROM project AS p1
    LEFT JOIN status AS s ON p1.statusid = s.statusid
) AS t ON c.customerid = t.customerid
WHERE (c.isdeleted <> TRUE OR (c.isdeleted IS NULL)) AND (c.isactive <> FALSE OR (c.isactive IS NULL))
ORDER BY c.customerid, p.paymenttermid, c0.currencyid, c1.cityid, t."ProjectId"

SELECT c.customerid, c.firstname, c.lastname, CASE
    WHEN c.companyname = '' THEN (COALESCE(c.firstname, '') || ' ') || COALESCE(c.lastname, '')
    ELSE c.companyname
END, (c.companylogourl IS NULL) OR c.companylogourl = '', c.companylogourl, c.pannumber, c.gstnumber, c.companyemail, COALESCE(c.phone1, ''), COALESCE(c.address1, ''), COALESCE(c.zipcode, ''), p.paymenttermid IS NULL, p.paymenttermid, p.paymenttermname, c0.currencyid IS NULL, c0.currencyid, c0.currencyname, c1.cityid IS NULL, c1.cityid, c1.cityname, (
    SELECT count(*)::int
    FROM project AS p0
    WHERE c.customerid = p0.customerid), t."ProjectId", t."ProjectName", t."TotalEmployees", t."TotalAmount", t."ProjectStatus", t.statusid
FROM customer AS c
LEFT JOIN paymentterm AS p ON c.paymenttermid = p.paymenttermid
LEFT JOIN currency AS c0 ON c.currencyid = c0.currencyid
LEFT JOIN city AS c1 ON c.cityid = c1.cityid
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT p1.projectid AS "ProjectId", COALESCE(p1.projectname, '') AS "ProjectName", (
        SELECT count(*)::int
        FROM projectcontract AS p2
        INNER JOIN contractemployee AS c2 ON p2.contractid = c2.contractid
        WHERE p1.projectid = p2.projectid AND c2.categorysubstatusid IN (5, 6, 4, 3, 2) AND c2.contractid = COALESCE((
            SELECT p3.contractid
            FROM projectcontract AS p3
            WHERE p1.projectid = p3.projectid
            LIMIT 1), 0)) AS "TotalEmployees", (
        SELECT COALESCE(sum(p4.amount), 0.0)
        FROM projectcontract AS p4
        WHERE p1.projectid = p4.projectid) AS "TotalAmount", s.statusname AS "ProjectStatus", s.statusid, p1.customerid
    FROM project AS p1
    LEFT JOIN status AS s ON p1.statusid = s.statusid
) AS t ON c.customerid = t.customerid
WHERE (c.isdeleted <> TRUE OR (c.isdeleted IS NULL)) AND (c.isactive <> FALSE OR (c.isactive IS NULL))
ORDER BY c.customerid, p.paymenttermid, c0.currencyid, c1.cityid, t."ProjectId"

SELECT c.customerid, c.firstname, c.lastname, CASE
    WHEN c.companyname = '' THEN (COALESCE(c.firstname, '') || ' ') || COALESCE(c.lastname, '')
    ELSE c.companyname
END, (c.companylogourl IS NULL) OR c.companylogourl = '', c.companylogourl, c.pannumber, c.gstnumber, c.companyemail, COALESCE(c.phone1, ''), COALESCE(c.address1, ''), COALESCE(c.zipcode, ''), p.paymenttermid IS NULL, p.paymenttermid, p.paymenttermname, c0.currencyid IS NULL, c0.currencyid, c0.currencyname, c1.cityid IS NULL, c1.cityid, c1.cityname, (
    SELECT count(*)::int
    FROM project AS p0
    WHERE c.customerid = p0.customerid), t."ProjectId", t."ProjectName", t."TotalEmployees", t."TotalAmount", t."ProjectStatus", t.statusid
FROM customer AS c
LEFT JOIN paymentterm AS p ON c.paymenttermid = p.paymenttermid
LEFT JOIN currency AS c0 ON c.currencyid = c0.currencyid
LEFT JOIN city AS c1 ON c.cityid = c1.cityid
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT p1.projectid AS "ProjectId", COALESCE(p1.projectname, '') AS "ProjectName", (
        SELECT count(*)::int
        FROM projectcontract AS p2
        INNER JOIN contractemployee AS c2 ON p2.contractid = c2.contractid
        WHERE p1.projectid = p2.projectid AND c2.categorysubstatusid IN (5, 6, 4, 3, 2) AND c2.contractid = COALESCE((
            SELECT p3.contractid
            FROM projectcontract AS p3
            WHERE p1.projectid = p3.projectid
            LIMIT 1), 0)) AS "TotalEmployees", (
        SELECT COALESCE(sum(p4.amount), 0.0)
        FROM projectcontract AS p4
        WHERE p1.projectid = p4.projectid) AS "TotalAmount", s.statusname AS "ProjectStatus", s.statusid, p1.customerid
    FROM project AS p1
    LEFT JOIN status AS s ON p1.statusid = s.statusid
) AS t ON c.customerid = t.customerid
WHERE (c.isdeleted <> TRUE OR (c.isdeleted IS NULL)) AND (c.isactive <> FALSE OR (c.isactive IS NULL))
ORDER BY c.customerid, p.paymenttermid, c0.currencyid, c1.cityid, t."ProjectId"

FROM (
    SELECT c.customerid, CASE
        WHEN (c.firstname IS NULL) OR c.firstname = '' THEN c.companyname
        ELSE c.firstname
    END AS c, c.lastname, CASE
        WHEN c.companyname = '' THEN (COALESCE(c.firstname, '') || ' ') || COALESCE(c.lastname, '')
        ELSE c.companyname
    END AS c0, (c.companylogourl IS NULL) OR c.companylogourl = '' AS c1, c.companylogourl, c.pannumber, c.gstnumber, c.companyemail, COALESCE(c.phone2, '') AS c2, COALESCE(c.phone1, '') AS c3, COALESCE(c.address1, '') AS c4, COALESCE(c.address2, '') AS c5, COALESCE(c.zipcode, '') AS c6, COALESCE(c.countryregioncode, '') AS c7, p.paymenttermid IS NULL AS c8, p.paymenttermid, p.paymenttermname, c0.currencyid IS NULL AS c9, c0.currencyid, c0.currencyname, c1.cityid IS NULL AS c10, c1.cityid, c1.cityname, s.stateid IS NULL AS c11, c1.stateid, s.statename, c2.countryid IS NULL AS c12, s.countryid, c2.countryname, (
        SELECT count(*)::int
        FROM project AS p0
        WHERE c.customerid = p0.customerid) AS c13, c.customercode, s.stateid AS stateid0, c2.countryid AS countryid0
    FROM customer AS c
    LEFT JOIN paymentterm AS p ON c.paymenttermid = p.paymenttermid
    LEFT JOIN currency AS c0 ON c.currencyid = c0.currencyid
    LEFT JOIN city AS c1 ON c.cityid = c1.cityid
    LEFT JOIN state AS s ON c1.stateid = s.stateid
    LEFT JOIN country AS c2 ON s.countryid = c2.countryid
    WHERE (c.isdeleted <> TRUE OR (c.isdeleted IS NULL)) AND (c.isactive <> FALSE OR (c.isactive IS NULL)) AND c.customerid = @__CustomerId_2
    LIMIT 1
) AS t
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT p1.projectid, COALESCE(p1.projectname, '') AS c, (
        SELECT count(*)::int
        FROM projectcontract AS p4
        INNER JOIN contractemployee AS c3 ON p4.contractid = c3.contractid
        WHERE p1.projectid = p4.projectid AND c3.categorysubstatusid IN (5, 6, 4, 3, 2) AND c3.contractid = COALESCE((
            SELECT p6.contractid
            FROM projectcontract AS p6
            WHERE p1.projectid = p6.projectid
            LIMIT 1), 0)) AS c0, (
        SELECT COALESCE(sum(p7.amount), 0.0)
        FROM projectcontract AS p7
        WHERE p1.projectid = p7.projectid) AS c1, p2.projecttypename, s0.subpracticename, p3.practicename, s1.statusname, p2.projecttypeid, s0.subpracticeid, p3.practiceid, s1.statusid, p5.contractstartdate, p5.contractenddate, p5.amount, p5.contractid, p1.customerid
    FROM project AS p1
    LEFT JOIN projecttype AS p2 ON p1.projecttypeid = p2.projecttypeid
    LEFT JOIN subpractice AS s0 ON p1.subpracticeid = s0.subpracticeid
    LEFT JOIN practice AS p3 ON s0.practiceid = p3.practiceid
    LEFT JOIN status AS s1 ON p1.statusid = s1.statusid
    LEFT JOIN projectcontract AS p5 ON p1.projectid = p5.projectid
) AS t0 ON t.customerid = t0.customerid

SELECT c.customerid, c.firstname, c.lastname, CASE
    WHEN c.companyname = '' THEN (COALESCE(c.firstname, '') || ' ') || COALESCE(c.lastname, '')
    ELSE c.companyname
END, (c.companylogourl IS NULL) OR c.companylogourl = '', c.companylogourl, c.pannumber, c.gstnumber, c.companyemail, COALESCE(c.phone1, ''), COALESCE(c.address1, ''), COALESCE(c.zipcode, ''), p.paymenttermid IS NULL, p.paymenttermid, p.paymenttermname, c0.currencyid IS NULL, c0.currencyid, c0.currencyname, c1.cityid IS NULL, c1.cityid, c1.cityname, (
    SELECT count(*)::int
    FROM project AS p0
    WHERE c.customerid = p0.customerid), t."ProjectId", t."ProjectName", t."TotalEmployees", t."TotalAmount", t."ProjectStatus", t.statusid
FROM customer AS c
LEFT JOIN paymentterm AS p ON c.paymenttermid = p.paymenttermid
LEFT JOIN currency AS c0 ON c.currencyid = c0.currencyid
LEFT JOIN city AS c1 ON c.cityid = c1.cityid
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT p1.projectid AS "ProjectId", COALESCE(p1.projectname, '') AS "ProjectName", (
        SELECT count(*)::int
        FROM projectcontract AS p2
        INNER JOIN contractemployee AS c2 ON p2.contractid = c2.contractid
        WHERE p1.projectid = p2.projectid AND c2.categorysubstatusid IN (5, 6, 4, 3, 2) AND c2.contractid = COALESCE((
            SELECT p3.contractid
            FROM projectcontract AS p3
            WHERE p1.projectid = p3.projectid
            LIMIT 1), 0)) AS "TotalEmployees", (
        SELECT COALESCE(sum(p4.amount), 0.0)
        FROM projectcontract AS p4
        WHERE p1.projectid = p4.projectid) AS "TotalAmount", s.statusname AS "ProjectStatus", s.statusid, p1.customerid
    FROM project AS p1
    LEFT JOIN status AS s ON p1.statusid = s.statusid
) AS t ON c.customerid = t.customerid
WHERE (c.isdeleted <> TRUE OR (c.isdeleted IS NULL)) AND (c.isactive <> FALSE OR (c.isactive IS NULL))
ORDER BY c.customerid, p.paymenttermid, c0.currencyid, c1.cityid, t."ProjectId"

SELECT c.customerid, c.firstname, c.lastname, CASE
    WHEN c.companyname = '' THEN (COALESCE(c.firstname, '') || ' ') || COALESCE(c.lastname, '')
    ELSE c.companyname
END, (c.companylogourl IS NULL) OR c.companylogourl = '', c.companylogourl, c.pannumber, c.gstnumber, c.companyemail, COALESCE(c.phone1, ''), COALESCE(c.address1, ''), COALESCE(c.zipcode, ''), p.paymenttermid IS NULL, p.paymenttermid, p.paymenttermname, c0.currencyid IS NULL, c0.currencyid, c0.currencyname, c1.cityid IS NULL, c1.cityid, c1.cityname, (
    SELECT count(*)::int
    FROM project AS p0
    WHERE c.customerid = p0.customerid), t."ProjectId", t."ProjectName", t."TotalEmployees", t."TotalAmount", t."ProjectStatus", t.statusid
FROM customer AS c
LEFT JOIN paymentterm AS p ON c.paymenttermid = p.paymenttermid
LEFT JOIN currency AS c0 ON c.currencyid = c0.currencyid
LEFT JOIN city AS c1 ON c.cityid = c1.cityid
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT p1.projectid AS "ProjectId", COALESCE(p1.projectname, '') AS "ProjectName", (
        SELECT count(*)::int
        FROM projectcontract AS p2
        INNER JOIN contractemployee AS c2 ON p2.contractid = c2.contractid
        WHERE p1.projectid = p2.projectid AND c2.categorysubstatusid IN (5, 6, 4, 3, 2) AND c2.contractid = COALESCE((
            SELECT p3.contractid
            FROM projectcontract AS p3
            WHERE p1.projectid = p3.projectid
            LIMIT 1), 0)) AS "TotalEmployees", (
        SELECT COALESCE(sum(p4.amount), 0.0)
        FROM projectcontract AS p4
        WHERE p1.projectid = p4.projectid) AS "TotalAmount", s.statusname AS "ProjectStatus", s.statusid, p1.customerid
    FROM project AS p1
    LEFT JOIN status AS s ON p1.statusid = s.statusid
) AS t ON c.customerid = t.customerid
WHERE (c.isdeleted <> TRUE OR (c.isdeleted IS NULL)) AND (c.isactive <> FALSE OR (c.isactive IS NULL))
ORDER BY c.customerid, p.paymenttermid, c0.currencyid, c1.cityid, t."ProjectId"

SELECT t.customerid, t.c, t.lastname, t.c0, t.c1, t.companylogourl, t.pannumber, t.gstnumber, t.companyemail, t.c2, t.c3, t.c4, t.c5, t.c6, t.c7, t.c8, t.paymenttermid, t.paymenttermname, t.c9, t.currencyid, t.currencyname, t.c10, t.cityid, t.cityname, t.c11, t.stateid, t.statename, t.c12, t.countryid, t.countryname, t.c13, t.stateid0, t.countryid0, t0.projectid, t0.c, t0.c0, t0.c1, t0.projecttypename, t0.subpracticename, t0.practicename, t0.statusname, t0.projecttypeid, t0.subpracticeid, t0.practiceid, t0.statusid, t0.contractstartdate, t0.contractenddate, t0.amount, t0.contractid, t.customercode
FROM (
    SELECT c.customerid, CASE
        WHEN (c.firstname IS NULL) OR c.firstname = '' THEN c.companyname
        ELSE c.firstname
    END AS c, c.lastname, CASE
        WHEN c.companyname = '' THEN (COALESCE(c.firstname, '') || ' ') || COALESCE(c.lastname, '')
        ELSE c.companyname
    END AS c0, (c.companylogourl IS NULL) OR c.companylogourl = '' AS c1, c.companylogourl, c.pannumber, c.gstnumber, c.companyemail, COALESCE(c.phone2, '') AS c2, COALESCE(c.phone1, '') AS c3, COALESCE(c.address1, '') AS c4, COALESCE(c.address2, '') AS c5, COALESCE(c.zipcode, '') AS c6, COALESCE(c.countryregioncode, '') AS c7, p.paymenttermid IS NULL AS c8, p.paymenttermid, p.paymenttermname, c0.currencyid IS NULL AS c9, c0.currencyid, c0.currencyname, c1.cityid IS NULL AS c10, c1.cityid, c1.cityname, s.stateid IS NULL AS c11, c1.stateid, s.statename, c2.countryid IS NULL AS c12, s.countryid, c2.countryname, (
        SELECT count(*)::int
        FROM project AS p0
        WHERE c.customerid = p0.customerid) AS c13, c.customercode, s.stateid AS stateid0, c2.countryid AS countryid0
    FROM customer AS c
    LEFT JOIN paymentterm AS p ON c.paymenttermid = p.paymenttermid
    LEFT JOIN currency AS c0 ON c.currencyid = c0.currencyid
    LEFT JOIN city AS c1 ON c.cityid = c1.cityid
    LEFT JOIN state AS s ON c1.stateid = s.stateid
    LEFT JOIN country AS c2 ON s.countryid = c2.countryid
    WHERE (c.isdeleted <> TRUE OR (c.isdeleted IS NULL)) AND (c.isactive <> FALSE OR (c.isactive IS NULL)) AND c.customerid = @__CustomerId_2
    LIMIT 1
) AS t
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT p1.projectid, COALESCE(p1.projectname, '') AS c, (
        SELECT count(*)::int
        FROM projectcontract AS p4
        INNER JOIN contractemployee AS c3 ON p4.contractid = c3.contractid
        WHERE p1.projectid = p4.projectid AND c3.categorysubstatusid IN (5, 6, 4, 3, 2) AND c3.contractid = COALESCE((
            SELECT p6.contractid
            FROM projectcontract AS p6
            WHERE p1.projectid = p6.projectid
            LIMIT 1), 0)) AS c0, (
        SELECT COALESCE(sum(p7.amount), 0.0)
        FROM projectcontract AS p7
        WHERE p1.projectid = p7.projectid) AS c1, p2.projecttypename, s0.subpracticename, p3.practicename, s1.statusname, p2.projecttypeid, s0.subpracticeid, p3.practiceid, s1.statusid, p5.contractstartdate, p5.contractenddate, p5.amount, p5.contractid, p1.customerid
    FROM project AS p1
    LEFT JOIN projecttype AS p2 ON p1.projecttypeid = p2.projecttypeid
    LEFT JOIN subpractice AS s0 ON p1.subpracticeid = s0.subpracticeid
    LEFT JOIN practice AS p3 ON s0.practiceid = p3.practiceid
    LEFT JOIN status AS s1 ON p1.statusid = s1.statusid
    LEFT JOIN projectcontract AS p5 ON p1.projectid = p5.projectid
) AS t0 ON t.customerid = t0.customerid
ORDER BY t.customerid, t.paymenttermid, t.currencyid, t.cityid, t.stateid0, t.countryid0, t0.projectid, t0.projecttypeid, t0.subpracticeid, t0.practiceid, t0.statusid
